dvipadī ॥ 1 ॥
itaḥ paraṁ dvipadyēō'dhikriyantē ॥ 1 ॥
dādālācadāli karpūrō ṇaiḥ ॥ 2 ॥

" ghaṇasāru mēlli kuṁkuma cayahi, parai karahi mayanāhi vi ।

kēcillaghvaṣṭakādārabhya laghudvayadrathavr̥ddhyā " vāhādīn bhēdānāhuḥ । yathāha--
bāhō vēhō' vaggō baṁdhū bāṇō va varō vēsō ।
